Section LaxSliceCleaving.
  Context {B : bicat}
          (a : B).

  (**
   1.1. Characterization of opcartesian 2-cells
   *)
  
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₁
t₂: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₂
ss₁: t₁ -->[ s₁] t₂
ss₂: t₁ -->[ s₂] t₂
αα: ss₁ ==>[ α] ss₂
is_opcartesian_2cell (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) αα

  
B: bicat

s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧

t₁: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₁
t₂: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₂

ss₂: t₁ -->[ s₂] t₂
αα: ss₁ ==>[ α] ss₂
is_opcartesian_2cell (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) αα

    
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₁
t₂: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₂
ss₁: t₁ -->[ s₁] t₂
ss₂: t₁ -->[ s₂] t₂
αα: ss₁ ==>[ α] ss₂
s₃: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
ss₃: t₁ -->[ s₃] t₂
γ: s₂ ==> s₃
γα: ss₁ ==>[ α • γ] ss₃
∃! γγ : ss₂ ==>[ γ] ss₃, αα •• γγ = γα

    
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₁
t₂: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₂

isaprop (∑ γγ : ss₂ ==>[ γ] ss₃, αα •• γγ = γα)

B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B

α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₁

γα: ss₁ ==>[ α • γ] ss₃
∏ x y : ss₂ ==>[ γ] ss₃,
(λ x0 : ss₂ ==>[ γ] ss₃, αα •• x0 = γα) x
→ (λ x0 : ss₂ ==>[ γ] ss₃, αα •• x0 = γα) y → x = y

x, y: ss₂ ==>[ γ] ss₃
X: (λ x : ss₂ ==>[ γ] ss₃, αα •• x = γα) x
X0: (λ x : ss₂ ==>[ γ] ss₃, αα •• x = γα) y
x = y

        apply cellset_property.

a, c₁, c₂: B

B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
ss₁: t₁ ==> s₁ · t₂
ss₂: t₁ ==> s₂ · t₂
αα: ss₁ • (α ▹ t₂) = ss₂
s₃: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
ss₃: t₁ ==> s₃ · t₂
γ: s₂ ==> s₃
γα: ss₁ • ((α • γ) ▹ t₂) = ss₃
ss₂ • (γ ▹ t₂) = ss₃

        
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
ss₁: t₁ ==> s₁ · t₂
ss₂: t₁ ==> s₂ · t₂
αα: ss₁ • (α ▹ t₂) = ss₂
s₃: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
ss₃: t₁ ==> s₃ · t₂
γ: s₂ ==> s₃
γα: ss₁ • ((α • γ) ▹ t₂) = ss₃
(ss₁ • (α ▹ t₂)) • (γ ▹ t₂) = ss₁ • ((α • γ) ▹ t₂)

        
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
ss₁: t₁ ==> s₁ · t₂
ss₂: t₁ ==> s₂ · t₂
αα: ss₁ • (α ▹ t₂) = ss₂
s₃: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
ss₃: t₁ ==> s₃ · t₂
γ: s₂ ==> s₃
γα: ss₁ • ((α • γ) ▹ t₂) = ss₃
ss₁ • ((α ▹ t₂) • (γ ▹ t₂)) = ss₁ • ((α • γ) ▹ t₂)

        
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
ss₁: t₁ ==> s₁ · t₂
ss₂: t₁ ==> s₂ · t₂
αα: ss₁ • (α ▹ t₂) = ss₂
s₃: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
ss₃: t₁ ==> s₃ · t₂
γ: s₂ ==> s₃
γα: ss₁ • ((α • γ) ▹ t₂) = ss₃
(α ▹ t₂) • (γ ▹ t₂) = (α • γ) ▹ t₂

        
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
ss₁: t₁ ==> s₁ · t₂
ss₂: t₁ ==> s₂ · t₂
αα: ss₁ • (α ▹ t₂) = ss₂
s₃: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
ss₃: t₁ ==> s₃ · t₂
γ: s₂ ==> s₃
γα: ss₁ • ((α • γ) ▹ t₂) = ss₃
(α • γ) ▹ t₂ = (α • γ) ▹ t₂

        apply idpath.
      
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₁
t₂: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₂
ss₁: t₁ -->[ s₁] t₂
ss₂: t₁ -->[ s₂] t₂
αα: ss₁ ==>[ α] ss₂
s₃: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
ss₃: t₁ -->[ s₃] t₂
γ: s₂ ==> s₃
γα: ss₁ ==>[ α • γ] ss₃
(λ γγ : ss₂ ==>[ γ] ss₃, αα •• γγ = γα)
  (internal_paths_rew (t₁ ==> s₃ · t₂)
     (ss₁ • ((α • γ) ▹ t₂))
     (λ ss₃ : t₁ ==> s₃ · t₂, ss₂ • (γ ▹ t₂) = ss₃)
     (internal_paths_rew (t₁ ==> s₂ · t₂)
        (ss₁ • (α ▹ t₂))
        (λ ss₂ : t₁ ==> s₂ · t₂,
         ss₂ • (γ ▹ t₂) = ss₁ • ((α • γ) ▹ t₂))
        (internal_paths_rew_r (t₁ ==> s₃ · t₂)
           ((ss₁ • (α ▹ t₂)) • (γ ▹ t₂))
           (ss₁ • ((α ▹ t₂) • (γ ▹ t₂)))
           (λ p : t₁ ==> s₃ · t₂,
            p = ss₁ • ((α • γ) ▹ t₂))
           (maponpaths (vcomp2 ss₁)
              (internal_paths_rew_r
                 (s₁ · t₂ ==> s₃ · t₂)
                 ((α ▹ t₂) • (γ ▹ t₂)) ((α • γ) ▹ t₂)
                 (λ p : s₁ · t₂ ==> s₃ · t₂,
                  p = (α • γ) ▹ t₂)
                 (idpath ((α • γ) ▹ t₂))
                 (rwhisker_vcomp t₂ α γ)))
           (vassocl ss₁ (α ▹ t₂) (γ ▹ t₂))) ss₂ αα)
     ss₃ γα
   :
   ss₂ ==>[ γ] ss₃)
 apply cellset_property.
  Qed.

  (**
   1.2. Local opcleaving and isocleaving
   *)

local_opcleaving (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a)

  
B: bicat
a: B
local_opcleaving (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a)

    
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: t₁ ==> s₁ · t₂
β: s₁ ==> s₂
opcartesian_lift_2cell (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) α β

    
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: t₁ ==> s₁ · t₂
β: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁ ==> s₂ · t₂
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: t₁ ==> s₁ · t₂
β: s₁ ==> s₂
∑ αα : α • (β ▹ t₂) = ?Goal,
is_opcartesian_2cell (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) αα

    
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: t₁ ==> s₁ · t₂
β: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁ ==> s₂ · t₂
 exact (α • (β ▹ t₂)).
    
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: t₁ ==> s₁ · t₂
β: s₁ ==> s₂
∑ αα : α • (β ▹ t₂) = α • (β ▹ t₂),
is_opcartesian_2cell (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) αα
 
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: t₁ ==> s₁ · t₂
β: s₁ ==> s₂
(λ αα : α • (β ▹ t₂) = α • (β ▹ t₂),
 is_opcartesian_2cell (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) αα)
  (idpath (α • (β ▹ t₂)))

      apply lax_slice_is_opcartesian_2cell.
  Defined.

∑ ff : s₁ ==> t₁ · s₂, disp_invertible_2cell β ff α

B: bicat

s₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
α: s₁ ==> t₂ · s₂
β: invertible_2cell t₁ t₂
(α • (β ^-1 ▹ s₂)) ==>[ β] α
 abstract
        (cbn ;
         rewrite !vassocl ;
         rewrite rwhisker_vcomp ;
         rewrite vcomp_linv ;
         rewrite id2_rwhisker ;
         apply id2_right).
    
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
t₁, t₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
s₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
s₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
α: s₁ ==> t₂ · s₂
β: invertible_2cell t₁ t₂
(λ x : (α • (β ^-1 ▹ s₂)) ==>[ β] α,
 is_disp_invertible_2cell β x)
  (lax_slice_local_iso_cleaving_subproof c₁ c₂ t₁ t₂
     s₁ s₂ α β)
 apply lax_slice_disp_locally_groupoid.
  Defined.

  (**
   1.3. Characterizations of cartesian 1-cells
   *)
  
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
t₁: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₁
t₂: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₂
ss: t₁ -->[ s] t₂
Hss: is_invertible_2cell ss
cartesian_1cell (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) ss

B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
t₁: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₁
t₂: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₂

((ss' • rassociator s' s t₂) • (s' ◃ Hss ^-1)) ;; ss ==>[
id2_invertible_2cell (s' · s)] ss'
 abstract
            (cbn ;
             rewrite id2_rwhisker ;
             rewrite id2_right ;
             rewrite !vassocl ;
             refine (_ @ id2_right _) ;
             apply maponpaths ;
             rewrite (maponpaths (λ z, _ • z) (vassocr _ _ _)) ;
             rewrite lwhisker_vcomp ;
             rewrite vcomp_linv ;
             rewrite lwhisker_id2 ;
             rewrite id2_left ;
             apply rassociator_lassociator).

  Lh'

B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧

Lh': lift_1cell_factor (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) ss αα
(λ δδ : Lh ==>[ β] Lh',
 transportf
   (λ z : s₁ · s ==> s₂ · s, Lh ;; ss ==>[ z] αα)
   (id2_right (β ▹ s) @ ! id2_left (β ▹ s))
   ((δδ ▹▹ ss)
    •• disp_cell_lift_1cell_factor
         (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) ss Lh') =
 disp_cell_lift_1cell_factor
   (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) ss Lh •• ββ) ?pr1

        
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
ss: t₁ ==> s · t₂
Hss: is_invertible_2cell ss
c₃: B
t₃: B ⟦ c₃, a ⟧
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₃, c₁ ⟧
α: t₃ ==> s₁ · s · t₂
αα: t₃ ==> s₂ · s · t₂
β: s₁ ==> s₂
ββ: α • ((β ▹ s) ▹ t₂) = αα
Lh: lift_1cell_factor (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) ss α
Lh': lift_1cell_factor (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) ss αα
Lh ==>[ β] Lh'
 abstract
            (pose (pr12 Lh') as p ;
             cbn in p ;
             rewrite id2_rwhisker in p ;
             rewrite id2_right in p ;
             use (vcomp_rcancel (s₂ ◃ ss)) ; [ is_iso ; apply Hss | ] ;
             use (vcomp_rcancel (lassociator _ _ _)) ; [ is_iso | ] ;
             refine (_ @ !p) ; clear p ;
             rewrite !vassocl ;
             pose (pr12 Lh) as p ;
             refine (_ @ ββ) ;
             cbn in p ;
             rewrite id2_rwhisker in p ;
             rewrite id2_right in p ;
             refine (_ @ maponpaths (λ z, z • _) p) ;
             rewrite !vassocl ;
             apply maponpaths ;
             rewrite !vassocr ;
             rewrite vcomp_whisker ;
             rewrite !vassocl ;
             rewrite rwhisker_rwhisker ;
             apply idpath).

d: pr1 p • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss) = linvunitor (s · t₂)
lift2: (ss • linvunitor (s · t₂))
• lassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ =
(ss • linvunitor (s · t₂))
• lassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
→ ∏
  Lh
   Lh' : lift_1cell_factor
           (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) ss
           ((ss • linvunitor (s · t₂))
            • lassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂),
  Lh • id₂ (id₁ c₁ · t₁) = Lh'
l':= lift2
  (idpath

      • lassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂)): ∏

          • lassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂),
Lh • id₂ (id₁ c₁ · t₁) = Lh'
(ss • pr1 p) • lunitor t₁ = id₂ t₁

t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
ss: t₁ ==> s · t₂
Hss: cartesian_1cell (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a) ss
p:= pr1 Hss c₁ (s · t₂) (id₁ c₁)
  (linvunitor (s · t₂) • lassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂): ∑ hh : s · t₂ ==> id₁ c₁ · t₁,

  (id2_invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁ · s))
  ((hh • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss))
   • lassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂)
  (linvunitor (s · t₂) • lassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂)
d: pr1 p • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss) = linvunitor (s · t₂)
lift2: (ss • linvunitor (s · t₂))
• lassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ =
(ss • linvunitor (s · t₂))
• lassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂

a, c₁, c₂: B
t₁: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₂
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
cartesian_1cell (lax_slice_disp_bicat B a)
  (id₂ (s · t₁))

    
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
t₁: lax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₂
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
is_invertible_2cell (id₂ (s · t₁))

    is_iso.
  Defined.
End LaxSliceCleaving.

  Context {B : bicat}

        apply cellset_property.

a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂

B: bicat

B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧

αα: (α ▹ t₂) • ss₂ = ss₁
s₃: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
ss₃: s₃ · t₂ ==> t₁
γ: s₃ ==> s₁
γα: ((γ • α) ▹ t₂) • ss₂ = ss₃
(γ ▹ t₂) • (α ▹ t₂) = (γ • α) ▹ t₂

        
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
ss₁: s₁ · t₂ ==> t₁
ss₂: s₂ · t₂ ==> t₁
αα: (α ▹ t₂) • ss₂ = ss₁
s₃: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
ss₃: s₃ · t₂ ==> t₁
γ: s₃ ==> s₁
γα: ((γ • α) ▹ t₂) • ss₂ = ss₃
(γ • α) ▹ t₂ = (γ • α) ▹ t₂

        apply idpath.
      
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
α: s₁ ==> s₂
t₁: oplax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₁
t₂: oplax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₂
ss₁: t₁ -->[ s₁] t₂
ss₂: t₁ -->[ s₂] t₂
αα: ss₁ ==>[ α] ss₂
s₃: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
ss₃: t₁ -->[ s₃] t₂
γ: s₃ ==> s₁
γα: ss₃ ==>[ γ • α] ss₂
(λ γγ : ss₃ ==>[ γ] ss₁, γγ •• αα = γα)
  (internal_paths_rew (s₁ · t₂ ==> t₁)
     ((α ▹ t₂) • ss₂)
     (λ ss₁ : s₁ · t₂ ==> t₁, (γ ▹ t₂) • ss₁ = ss₃)
     (internal_paths_rew (s₃ · t₂ ==> t₁)
        (((γ • α) ▹ t₂) • ss₂)
        (λ ss₃ : s₃ · t₂ ==> t₁,
         (γ ▹ t₂) • ((α ▹ t₂) • ss₂) = ss₃)
        (internal_paths_rew_r (s₃ · t₂ ==> t₁)
           ((γ ▹ t₂) • ((α ▹ t₂) • ss₂))
           (((γ ▹ t₂) • (α ▹ t₂)) • ss₂)
           (λ p : s₃ · t₂ ==> t₁,
            p = ((γ • α) ▹ t₂) • ss₂)
           (maponpaths_2 vcomp2
              (internal_paths_rew_r
                 (s₃ · t₂ ==> s₂ · t₂)
                 ((γ ▹ t₂) • (α ▹ t₂)) ((γ • α) ▹ t₂)
                 (λ p : s₃ · t₂ ==> s₂ · t₂,
                  p = (γ • α) ▹ t₂)
                 (idpath ((γ • α) ▹ t₂))
                 (rwhisker_vcomp t₂ γ α)) ss₂)
           (vassocr (γ ▹ t₂) (α ▹ t₂) ss₂)) ss₃ γα)
     ss₁ αα
   :
   ss₃ ==>[ γ] ss₁)
 apply cellset_property.
  Qed.

is_cartesian_2cell (oplax_slice_disp_bicat B a) αα

∑ αα : (β ▹ t₂) • α = (β ▹ t₂) • α,
is_cartesian_2cell (oplax_slice_disp_bicat B a) αα
 
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B

(λ αα : (β ▹ t₂) • α = (β ▹ t₂) • α,
 is_cartesian_2cell (oplax_slice_disp_bicat B a) αα)
  (idpath ((β ▹ t₂) • α))

      apply oplax_slice_is_cartesian_2cell.
  Defined.

  (**
   2.3. Characterizations of cartesian 1-cells
   *)
  
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
t₁: oplax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₁

s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
ss: s · t₂ ==> t₁
Hss: cartesian_1cell (oplax_slice_disp_bicat B a) ss
p:= pr1 Hss c₁ (s · t₂) (id₁ c₁)
  (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • lunitor (s · t₂)): ∑ hh : s · t₂ -->[ id₁ c₁] t₁,
disp_invertible_2cell
  (id2_invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁ · s)) (hh ;; ss)
  (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • lunitor (s · t₂))
is_invertible_2cell ss

disp_invertible_2cell
  (id2_invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁ · s)) (hh ;; ss)
  (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • lunitor (s · t₂))
d:= pr12 p: pr1 p ;; ss ==>[
id2_invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁ · s)] (rassociator
                                      (id₁ c₁) s
                                      t₂
                                    • lunitor
                                        (s · t₂))

a, c₁, c₂: B
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧

t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧

  (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • lunitor (s · t₂))
d:= pr12 p: (id₂ (id₁ c₁ · s) ▹ t₂)
• (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • lunitor (s · t₂)) =
(rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss))
• pr1 p
is_invertible_2cell ss

  (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • lunitor (s · t₂))
d: rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • lunitor (s · t₂) =
(rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss))
• pr1 p
id₂ (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂) • (lunitor s ▹ t₂) =
lunitor s ▹ t₂

 is_disp_invertible_2cell
   (id2_invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁ · s)) x)
  (internal_paths_rew_r
     (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> id₁ c₁ · s · t₂)
     (id₂ (id₁ c₁ · s) ▹ t₂) (id₂ (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂))
     (λ p : id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> id₁ c₁ · s · t₂,
      p
      • ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • lunitor (s · t₂))
         • ss) =
      (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss))
      • lunitor t₁)
     (internal_paths_rew_r (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> t₁)
        (id₂ (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂)
         • ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
             • lunitor (s · t₂)) • ss))
        ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • lunitor (s · t₂))
         • ss)
        (λ p : id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> t₁,
         p =
         (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss))
         • lunitor t₁)
        (internal_paths_rew_r (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> t₁)
           ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
             • lunitor (s · t₂)) • ss)
           (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
            • (lunitor (s · t₂) • ss))
           (λ p : id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> t₁,
            p =
            (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss))
            • lunitor t₁)
           (internal_paths_rew_r
              (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> t₁)
              ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
                • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss)) • lunitor t₁)
              (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
               • ((id₁ c₁ ◃ ss) • lunitor t₁))
              (λ p : id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> t₁,
               rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
               • (lunitor (s · t₂) • ss) = p)
              (maponpaths
                 (vcomp2 (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂))
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (id₁ c₁ · (s · t₂) ==> t₁)
                    ((id₁ c₁ ◃ ss) • lunitor t₁)
                    (lunitor (s · t₂) • ss)
                    (λ p : id₁ c₁ · (s · t₂) ==> t₁,
                     lunitor (s · t₂) • ss = p)
                    (idpath (lunitor (s · t₂) • ss))
                    (vcomp_lunitor (s · t₂) t₁ ss)))
              (vassocl (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂)
                 (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss) (lunitor t₁)))
           (vassocl (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂)
              (lunitor (s · t₂)) ss))
        (id2_left
           ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
             • lunitor (s · t₂)) • ss)))
     (id2_rwhisker (id₁ c₁ · s) t₂)
   :
   ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss))
    • lunitor t₁) ==>[
   id2_invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁ · s)] ((rassociator
                                          (id₁ c₁) s
                                          t₂
                                        • lunitor
                                            (s · t₂))

                                              (id₁ c₁)
                                              s t₂
                                            • lunitor
                                                (s
                                                 · t₂))
                                           • ss),
 is_disp_invertible_2cell
   (id2_invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁ · s)) x)
  (internal_paths_rew_r
     (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> id₁ c₁ · s · t₂)
     (id₂ (id₁ c₁ · s) ▹ t₂) (id₂ (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂))
     (λ p0 : id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> id₁ c₁ · s · t₂,
      p0
      • ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • lunitor (s · t₂))
         • ss) =
      (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss))
      • (pr1 p • ss))
     (internal_paths_rew_r (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> t₁)
        (id₂ (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂)
         • ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
             • lunitor (s · t₂)) • ss))
        ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • lunitor (s · t₂))
         • ss)
        (λ p0 : id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> t₁,
         p0 =
         (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss))
         • (pr1 p • ss))
        (internal_paths_rew_r (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> t₁)
           ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss))
            • (pr1 p • ss))
           (((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
              • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss)) • pr1 p) • ss)
           (λ p : id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> t₁,
            (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
             • lunitor (s · t₂)) • ss = p)
           (maponpaths_2 vcomp2
              (internal_paths_rew_r
                 (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> s · t₂)
                 ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
                   • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss)) • pr1 p)
                 (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
                  • ((id₁ c₁ ◃ ss) • pr1 p))
                 (λ p : id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> s · t₂,
                  rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
                  • lunitor (s · t₂) = p)
                 (internal_paths_rew_r
                    (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> s · t₂)
                    (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
                     • lunitor (s · t₂))
                    ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
                      • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss)) • pr1 p)
                    (λ p0 : id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> s · t₂,
                     p0 =
                     rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
                     • ((id₁ c₁ ◃ ss) • pr1 p))
                    (internal_paths_rew_r
                       (id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==> s · t₂)
                       ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
                         • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss)) • pr1 p)
                       (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
                        • ((id₁ c₁ ◃ ss) • pr1 p))
                       (λ p0 : id₁ c₁ · s · t₂ ==>
                               s · t₂,
                        p0 =
                        rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
                        • ((id₁ c₁ ◃ ss) • pr1 p))
                       (idpath
                          (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
                           • ((id₁ c₁ ◃ ss) • pr1 p)))
                       (vassocl
                          (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂)
                          (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss) (pr1 p))) d)
                 (vassocl (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂)
                    (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss) (pr1 p))) ss)
           (vassocr
              (rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
               • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss)) (pr1 p) ss))
        (id2_left
           ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂
             • lunitor (s · t₂)) • ss)))
     (id2_rwhisker (id₁ c₁ · s) t₂)
   :
   ((rassociator (id₁ c₁) s t₂ • (id₁ c₁ ◃ ss))
    • (pr1 p • ss)) ==>[
   id2_invertible_2cell (id₁ c₁ · s)] ((rassociator
                                          (id₁ c₁) s
                                          t₂
                                        • lunitor
                                            (s · t₂))
                                       • ss))
 apply oplax_slice_disp_locally_groupoid.
  Qed.

  (**
   2.4. Global cleaving
   *)

∑ (aa : oplax_slice_disp_bicat B a c₁)

  (id₂ (s · t₁))

    is_iso.
  Defined.
End OplaxSliceCleaving.

αα: invertible_2cell t₃ (s₂ · s · t₂)
β: s₁ ==> s₂
ββ: pr1 α • ((β ▹ s) ▹ t₂) = αα
Lh: lift_1cell_factor (slice_disp_bicat a) ss α
Lh': lift_1cell_factor (slice_disp_bicat a) ss αα
isaprop
  (lift_2cell_factor_type (slice_disp_bicat a) ss ββ
     Lh Lh')
 abstract
          (use invproofirrelevance ;
           intros φ₁ φ₂ ;
           use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply (slice_disp_bicat a) | ] ;
           apply cellset_property).

Lh: lift_1cell_factor (slice_disp_bicat a) ss α
Lh': lift_1cell_factor (slice_disp_bicat a) ss αα
lift_2cell_factor_type (slice_disp_bicat a) ss ββ Lh
  Lh'

B: bicat

(λ δδ : Lh ==>[ β] Lh',
 transportf
   (λ z : s₁ · s ==> s₂ · s, Lh ;; ss ==>[ z] αα)
   (id2_right (β ▹ s) @ ! id2_left (β ▹ s))
   ((δδ ▹▹ ss)
    •• disp_cell_lift_1cell_factor
         (slice_disp_bicat a) ss Lh') =
 disp_cell_lift_1cell_factor (slice_disp_bicat a) ss
   Lh •• ββ) ?pr1

        
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
ss: invertible_2cell t₁ (s · t₂)
c₃: B
t₃: B ⟦ c₃, a ⟧
s₁, s₂: B ⟦ c₃, c₁ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell t₃ (s₁ · s · t₂)
αα: invertible_2cell t₃ (s₂ · s · t₂)
β: s₁ ==> s₂
ββ: pr1 α • ((β ▹ s) ▹ t₂) = αα
Lh: lift_1cell_factor (slice_disp_bicat a) ss α
Lh': lift_1cell_factor (slice_disp_bicat a) ss αα
Lh ==>[ β] Lh'
 abstract
            (pose (pr12 Lh') as p ;
             cbn in p ;
             rewrite id2_rwhisker in p ;
             rewrite id2_right in p ;
             use (vcomp_rcancel (s₂ ◃ ss)) ; [ is_iso ; apply ss | ] ;
             use (vcomp_rcancel (lassociator _ _ _)) ; [ is_iso | ] ;
             rewrite !vassocl ;
             refine (_ @ !p) ; clear p ;
             pose (pr12 Lh) as p ;
             refine (_ @ ββ) ;
             cbn in p ;
             rewrite id2_rwhisker in p ;
             rewrite id2_right in p ;
             refine (_ @ maponpaths (λ z, z • _) p) ;
             rewrite !vassocl ;
             apply maponpaths ;
             rewrite !vassocr ;
             rewrite vcomp_whisker ;
             rewrite !vassocl ;
             rewrite rwhisker_rwhisker ;
             apply idpath).
        
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
t₁: B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧
t₂: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧

c₃: B

(λ δδ : Lh ==>[ β] Lh',
 transportf
   (λ z : s₁ · s ==> s₂ · s, Lh ;; ss ==>[ z] αα)
   (id2_right (β ▹ s) @ ! id2_left (β ▹ s))
   ((δδ ▹▹ ss)
    •• disp_cell_lift_1cell_factor
         (slice_disp_bicat a) ss Lh') =
 disp_cell_lift_1cell_factor (slice_disp_bicat a) ss
   Lh •• ββ)
  (slice_is_cartesian_1cell_subproof1 c₁ c₂ s t₁ t₂ ss
     c₃ t₃ s₁ s₂ α αα β ββ Lh Lh')
 apply cellset_property.
  Defined.

  (**
   3.3. Global cleaving
   *)
  
B: bicat
a: B
global_cleaving (slice_disp_bicat a)

  
B: bicat
a: B
global_cleaving (slice_disp_bicat a)

    
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
t₁: slice_disp_bicat a c₂
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
∑ (aa : slice_disp_bicat a c₁) (ff : aa -->[ s] t₁),
cartesian_1cell (slice_disp_bicat a) ff

    
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
t₁: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
∑ (aa : B ⟦ c₁, a ⟧)
(ff : invertible_2cell aa (s · t₁)),
cartesian_1cell (slice_disp_bicat a) ff

    
B: bicat
a, c₁, c₂: B
t₁: B ⟦ c₂, a ⟧
s: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
cartesian_1cell (slice_disp_bicat a)
  (id2_invertible_2cell (s · t₁))

    apply slice_is_cartesian_1cell.
  Defined.
End SliceCleaving.
